        function cdnfallback() {
            if (window.appInsights) {
                var region = "West Europe";
                var siteName = "acom-prod-westeurope-02";
                var error = new Error('Bundle - client side cdn fallback to local cdn, region: ' + region + ' , sitename: ' + siteName);

                window.appInsights.trackException({ exception: error });
            }

            if (window.location.search.indexOf('cdn=disable') === -1) {
                window.location.href = '?cdn=disable';
            }
        }

  <script>

    $(window).on('load', function () {
        function enableSSO() {
            setTimeout(function () {
                window.addEventListener("message", receiveMessage, false);
                var iframe = document.createElement('iframe');
                iframe.src = '/auth/sso/';
                iframe.setAttribute('id', 'sso-frame');
                iframe.setAttribute('style', 'width: 0; height: 0; border: 0; border: none; position: absolute;');
                iframe.setAttribute('aria-hidden', true);
                $('body').prepend(iframe);
            }, 500);
        }

        function receiveMessage(event) {
            if (event.origin !== 'https://azure.microsoft.com' || event.data !== 'sso-success') {
            return;
            }

            
            window.setTimeout(function () { document.getElementById('sso-frame').contentWindow.location.replace('/auth/sso/'); }, 30 * 60 * 1000);

            
            var enabledSubmitInputs = $('input:enabled[type="submit"], button:enabled[type="submit"]');
            enabledSubmitInputs.attr('disabled', true);

            window.dispatchEvent(createNewEvent('sso.success')); 

            
            $.ajax({ url: '/auth/sso/info/', timeout: 3000 })
                .done(function (data) {
                    if (data) {
                        $('.auth-container').html(data);
                    }
                })
                .fail(function () {
                    
                    enabledSubmitInputs.attr('disabled', false);
                });

            
            $.ajax({ url: '/auth/antiforgerytoken/', timeout: 3000 })
                .done(function (data) {
                    $('input[name="__RequestVerificationToken"]').replaceWith(data);
                    window.dispatchEvent(createNewEvent('sso.requestVerificationTokenReceived'));
                })
                .always(function () {
                    
                    enabledSubmitInputs.attr('disabled', false);
                });
        }

        
        function createNewEvent(eventName) {
            var event;

            if (typeof (Event) === 'function') {
                event = new Event(eventName);
            } else {
                event = document.createEvent('Event'); 
                event.initEvent(eventName, true, true);
            }

            return event;
        }

        // We won't process requests made from any status page
        if (window.location.pathname.indexOf('/status/') === -1)
        {
            // enable sso only if the userAgent is not safari
            if (!/^((?!chrome|android).)*safari/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
                enableSSO();
            }
        }
    });

</script>

   <section class="section" aria-label="Conversational AI for healthcare" data-module="media-05">

      <div class="split-image"> 
       <div class="split-image__content"> 
        <div class="row column"> 
         <h2>Conversational AI for healthcare</h2> 
         <p>Azure Health Bot empowers developers in healthcare organizations to build and deploy AI-powered, compliant, conversational healthcare experiences at scale. It combines built-in medical databases with natural language capabilities to understand clinical terminology and support compliance requirements including HIPAA.</p>

       <div class="step-through__slide" data-tour="botservice" data-slide="slide1"> 
        <div class="step-through__step" data-tour="botservice" data-slide="slide1" data-step="step1"> 
         <div class="row row-size2"> 
          <div class="column medium-7 large-9"> 
           <img class="step-through__step-image" src="//azurecomcdn.azureedge.net/cvt-526390d16d87de1877250c5808f92a928069f41676f250913969acdedd7e9a4a/images/page/services/bot-services/index/botservice-slide1-step1.gif?637585610552419661" alt="" role="presentation"> 
          </div> 
          <div class="column medium-5 large-3"> 
           <div class="card card-size2 card--gray80 oneStep"> 
            <div class="step-through__step-control text-center"> <button type="button" class="step-through__prev-step" aria-label="Wstecz"></button> <span class="step-through__step-label">Krok 1 z 1</span> <button type="button" class="step-through__next-step" aria-label="Nast?pne"></button> 
            </div> 
            <p class="text-heading5">Step 1: Create an Azure Bot</p> 
            <p></p>
            <ul> 
             <li>Create a <a href="/pl-pl/free/">free Azure account</a>.</li> 
             <li>Select <b>Create a resource</b>.</li> 
             <li>Type "bot" and select <b>Azure Bot</b>.</li> 
             <li>Configure resources.</li> 
             <li>Your bot is created.</li> 
             <li>Select <b>Open in Composer</b> to start editing your bot.</li> 
            </ul>
            <p></p> 
           </div> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="step-through__slide" data-tour="botservice" data-slide="slide2"> 
        <div class="step-through__step" data-tour="botservice" data-slide="slide2" data-step="step1"> 
         <div class="row row-size2"> 
          <div class="column medium-7 large-9"> 
           <img class="step-through__step-image" src="//azurecomcdn.azureedge.net/cvt-526390d16d87de1877250c5808f92a928069f41676f250913969acdedd7e9a4a/images/page/services/bot-services/index/botservice-slide2-step1.gif?637585610552419661" alt="" role="presentation"> 
          </div> 
          <div class="column medium-5 large-3"> 
           <div class="card card-size2 card--gray80 oneStep"> 
            <div class="step-through__step-control text-center"> <button type="button" class="step-through__prev-step" aria-label="Wstecz"></button> <span class="step-through__step-label">Krok 1 z 1</span> <button type="button" class="step-through__next-step" aria-label="Nast?pne"></button> 
            </div> 
            <p class="text-heading5">Step 2: Design a sophisticated bot</p> 
            <p></p>
            <ul> 
             <li>Choose from a list of templates.</li> 
             <li>Design your bot's conversational logic.</li> 
             <li>Utilize open-source packages to extend your bot.</li> 
            </ul>
            <p></p> 
           </div> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="step-through__slide" data-tour="botservice" data-slide="slide3"> 
        <div class="step-through__step" data-tour="botservice" data-slide="slide3" data-step="step1"> 
         <div class="row row-size2"> 
          <div class="column medium-7 large-9"> 
           <img class="step-through__step-image" src="//azurecomcdn.azureedge.net/cvt-526390d16d87de1877250c5808f92a928069f41676f250913969acdedd7e9a4a/images/page/services/bot-services/index/botservice-slide3-step1.gif?637585610552419661" alt="" role="presentation"> 
          </div> 
          <div class="column medium-5 large-3"> 
           <div class="card card-size2 card--gray80 oneStep"> 
            <div class="step-through__step-control text-center"> <button type="button" class="step-through__prev-step" aria-label="Wstecz"></button> <span class="step-through__step-label">Krok 1 z 1</span> <button type="button" class="step-through__next-step" aria-label="Nast?pne"></button> 
            </div> 
            <p class="text-heading5">Step 3: Select Connections and publish</p> 
            <p></p>
            <ul> 
             <li>Test and debug your bot in Bot Framework Composer.</li> 
             <li>Select <b>Connections</b>.</li> 
             <li>Provision and publish your bot from Bot Framework Composer.</li> 
            </ul>
            <p></p> 
           </div> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
   </section> 
   <section id="pricing" class="section section-size6" aria-label="Cennik us?ug Azure Bot Services" data-module="content-pricing-02"> 
    <div class="row row--middled-small"> 
     <div class="column medium-2 medium-offset-2"> 
      <img src="//azurecomcdn.azureedge.net/cvt-526390d16d87de1877250c5808f92a928069f41676f250913969acdedd7e9a4a/images/page/services/bot-services/index/pricing.svg" alt=""> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column medium-5 end"> 
      <div class="row column"> 
       <h2>Cennik us?ug Azure Bot Services</h2> 
       <p>Azure Bot Service is a managed bot development service that helps you seamlessly connect to your users via popular channels. Pay only for messages delivered using Premium channels, which allow your bot to communicate with users within your own application or on your website.</p>

   <section id="documentation" class="section" aria-label="Resources and documentation" data-module="content-documentation-01"> 
    <div class="row"> 
     <div class="column medium-3"> 
      <h2>Resources and documentation</h2> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column medium-3 end"> 
      <h3 class="text-heading4">Bot Framework Composer</h3> 
      <p>Get Bot Framework Composer for <a href="https://aka.ms/bf-composer-download-win">Windows</a>, <a href="https://aka.ms/bf-composer-download-mac">Mac</a>, or <a href="https://aka.ms/bf-composer-download-linux">Linux</a>.</p> 
      <p>Review <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/pl-pl/composer/introduction">Microsoft</a> and <a href="https://github.com/microsoft/BotFramework-Composer">GitHub</a> documentation.</p> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column medium-3 end"> 
      <h3 class="text-heading4">Samples and learning modules</h3> 
      <p><a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/pl-pl/learn/paths/create-bots-with-the-azure-bot-service/">Learn</a> how to build simple FAQ bots and intelligent, multiturn conversational experiences.</p> 
      <p>Explore and download <a href="https://github.com/Microsoft/BotBuilder-Samples">samples from GitHub</a>.</p> 
      <p>Read <a href="/pl-pl/resources/create-your-first-intelligent-bot-with-microsoft-ai/">A Developer's Guide to Building AI Applications</a>.</p> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column medium-3 end"> 
      <h3 class="text-heading4">Spo?eczno?? i pomoc techniczna</h3> 
      <p>Ask questions and get support from Microsoft engineers and the open-source Bot Framework community on <a href="https://gitter.im/Microsoft/BotBuilder">Gitter</a> and <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/botframework">StackOverflow</a>.</p> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
   </section>

   <section class="section" aria-label="Extend Power Virtual Agents with Azure" data-module="content-image-02"> 
    <div class="row"> 
     <div class="column medium-7"> 
      <img src="//azurecomcdn.azureedge.net/cvt-526390d16d87de1877250c5808f92a928069f41676f250913969acdedd7e9a4a/images/page/services/bot-services/index/extend-power.png" class="device-wrapper" alt=""> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column medium-5 large-4 large-offset-1"> 
      <h2>Extend Power Virtual Agents with Azure</h2> 
      <p>Extend bots built by subject-matter experts and business users in Microsoft Power Virtual Agents bots with Bot Framework Composer.</p> <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/pl-pl/power-virtual-agents/fundamentals-what-is-power-virtual-agents" class="arrow-link">Dowiedz si? wi?cej</a> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
   </section> 
   <section id="faq" class="section" aria-label="Cz?sto zadawane pytania dotycz?ce us?ug Azure Bot Services" data-module="faq-01"> 
    <div class="row"> 
     <div class="column medium-3"> 
      <h2>Cz?sto zadawane pytania dotycz?ce us?ug Azure Bot Services</h2> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column medium-8 medium-offset-1"> 
      <ul class="faq"> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="1bd5e232" data-bi-slot="1" data-bi-id="faq-1" data-bi-an="faq-01"> Where should I start? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="1bd5e232">
         <p><a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/pl-pl/azure/bot-service/bot-service-overview-introduction?view=azure-bot-service-4.0">Bot Framework</a> is a comprehensive conversational AI development environment for designing conversational AI experiences. <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/pl-pl/composer/introduction">Bot Framework Composer</a>, <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/pl-pl/azure/bot-service/?view=azure-bot-service-4.0">Azure Bot Service</a>, <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/pl-pl/azure/health-bot/overview">Azure Health Bot</a>, and <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/pl-pl/power-virtual-agents/fundamentals-what-is-power-virtual-agents">Power Virtual Agents</a> are built on Bot Framework.</p> 
         <p><a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/pl-pl/azure/cognitive-services/qnamaker/overview/overview">QnA Maker</a> is an Azure Cognitive Service that automatically extracts question-and- answer pairs from semi-structured documents, including website FAQ. QnA Maker makes it easy to create simple bots without the need to write code.</p> 
         <p><a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/pl-pl/azure/bot-service/?view=azure-bot-service-4.0">Azure Health Bot</a> is specifically designed to build bots for the healthcare domain. <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/pl-pl/power-virtual-agents/fundamentals-what-is-power-virtual-agents">Power Virtual Agents</a> is a no-code bot-building experience, available as a software as a service (SaaS) on <a href="https://powerplatform.microsoft.com/en-us/what-is-power-platform/">Microsoft Power Platform</a>.</p>
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="a413f78a" data-bi-slot="2" data-bi-id="faq-2" data-bi-an="faq-01"> What is Bot Framework Composer? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="a413f78a">
         <p><a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/pl-pl/composer/introduction">Bot Framework Composer</a> is a visual, open-source bot authoring canvas to build, test, and deploy bots directly to Azure. Start with a simple question-and-answer bot extracted from semi-structured documents or a website, or with prebuilt components that can be extended with code and logic to create sophisticated multilingual and multimodal bots for any scenario.</p> 
         <p>Bots built in Power Virtual Agents can be extended in Bot Framework Composer.</p>
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="652df652" data-bi-slot="3" data-bi-id="faq-3" data-bi-an="faq-01"> Can I use open-source software with Bot Framework? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="652df652">
         Yes. The Bot Framework SDKs and tools are all built as open-source technologies, available through the <a href="https://github.com/microsoft/botframework-sdk">GitHub repo</a>. In addition, you can integrate your own components and technologies in your bot solution as needed for your scenario.
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="715282e1" data-bi-slot="4" data-bi-id="faq-4" data-bi-an="faq-01"> Does Bot Framework provide analytics for my bot? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="715282e1">
         Yes. As a developer solution, Bot Framework provides designs that utilize <a href="/pl-pl/services/monitor/">Application Insights</a> to collect service-level and conversation-level data that can help gauge the performance and efficacy of your bot. Application Insights is available for bots built directly with the <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/pl-pl/azure/bot-service/bot-service-overview-introduction?view=azure-bot-service-4.0">Bot Framework SDK</a>, as well as <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/pl-pl/composer/introduction">Bot Framework Composer</a>.
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="eea79020" data-bi-slot="5" data-bi-id="faq-5" data-bi-an="faq-01"> Does Bot Framework include natural language AI and speech? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="eea79020">
         Yes. Bot Framework uses <a href="/pl-pl/services/cognitive-services/language-understanding-intelligent-service/">Language Understanding (LUIS)</a> for building custom machine-learning language models to extract information from conversational phrases and <a href="https://speech.microsoft.com/">Azure Speech</a> and <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/pl-pl/azure/cognitive-services/speech-service/direct-line-speech">Direct Line Speech</a> for creating intuitive and extensible voice-based interaction with bots.
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="b43a07ad" data-bi-slot="6" data-bi-id="faq-6" data-bi-an="faq-01"> Which languages are supported by Bot Framework? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="b43a07ad">
         <p>The Bot Framework SDK and Bot Framework Composer provide <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/pl-pl/composer/how-to-use-multiple-language">multilingual support</a> for bot development for a variety of languages, with English as the default.</p> 
         <p>The Bot Framework SDK supports multiple <a href="https://github.com/microsoft/botframework-sdk/#readme">programming languages</a>, including C#, JS, Python, and Java.</p> 
         <p><a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/pl-pl/composer/introduction">Bot Framework Composer</a> contains reusable assets in the form of JSON and Markdown files that can be bundled and packaged with a bot's source code, which can be checked into source control systems and deployed along with code updates such as dialogs, language understanding training data, and message templates.</p>
        </div> </li> 
      </ul> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
   </section>
